I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.33236*A┬▓ - 0.33236*A*exp(-0.07071*t) + 0.13650*sin(sqrt(A))`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `A┬▓` (polynomial)
2. `A*exp(╬▒t)` (exponential decay in t, linear in A)
3. `sin(sqrt(A))` (sinusoidal of square root)

The key distinguishing feature is `sin(sqrt(A))`. This is NOT equivalent to:
- `sqrt(A)` (linear in sqrt(A))
- `log(...)` functions
- `cos(A*c)` functions
- `A^c` power functions
- Rational functions of A
- `sin(A*c + d)` (sin of linear function of A, not sqrt)

Let me check each candidate for the presence of `sin(sqrt(A))` or something equivalent.

**Candidates 1-29, 31-37:** None contain `sin(sqrt(A))`. They contain combinations of `sqrt(A)`, `A^c`, `log(...)`, `cos(A*c)`, rational functions, `exp(A*c)`, `A^(1/3)`, etc. None of these can produce `sin(sqrt(A))`.

**Candidate 30:** `sqrt(A)*c0 + A┬▓*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6) + c7*log(A*c8+1)/sqrt(A)`
Contains `sin(A*c5 + c6)` which is `sin` of a linear function of A, not `sin(sqrt(A))`. These are different functions. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** `sqrt(A)*c0 + A┬▓*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5/(A+c6) + c7*sin(A*c8+c9)`
Contains `sin(A*c8+c9)`, not `sin(sqrt(A))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** `sqrt(A)*c0 + A┬▓*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8*exp(A*c9)`

**Candidate 49:** `sqrt(A)*c0 + A┬▓*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5/(A*c6+1) + c7*sin(A*c8+c9)`

**Candidate 55:** `A^(1/3)*c0 + A┬▓*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*|A|+1)+c9)`
Contains `sin(c7*log(c8*|A|+1)+c9)`. For AтЙе0, this is `sin(c7*log(c8*A+1)+c9)`. Can this equal `sin(sqrt(A))`? We'd need `c7*log(c8*A+1)+c9 = sqrt(A)` for all AтЙе0, but `log` and `sqrt` are linearly independent transcendental functions - they can't be equal for all A. Also has `exp(A*c5)` and `A^(1/3)` instead of the needed terms. **NO MATCH**
